***boventoon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boventoon.html>boventoon</a> (84584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boventoon.html>boventoon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boventonen.html>boventonen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boventoon.html>boventoontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***bowls.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bowls.html>bowls</a> (108578)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bowls.html>bowls</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">plural of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bowl</i></span></span></li>
<li>A precision sport where the goal <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> to roll biased <a href = vnd.unilang:balls.html>balls</a> (weighted on one side, and called <a href = vnd.unilang:bowls.html>bowls</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:closer.html>closer</a> to a <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> white ball (the <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:kitty.html>kitty</a>) than one's opponent <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> able to do.</li>
<li>A ball used in the game of <a href = vnd.unilang:bowls.html>bowls</a></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bowls.html>bowls</a></strong>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boycot.html>boycot</a> (27229)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">boycott</i>, originating from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Boycott" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Charles Boycott"><a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>Captain</a> Charles Cunningham Boycott</a>, an English evicting <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> in Ireland who <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> subject to a boycott organized by the Irish <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>Land</a> League in 1880.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:braaksel.html>braaksel</a> (15197)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:braken.html>braken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to vomit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-sel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a> indicating product of an action</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>

***brack.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brack.html>brack</a> (38477)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brak.html>brak</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brack.html>brack</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Salty or brackish water.
<ul><li><b>1627</b>:  "The Moone-Calfe" by Michael Drayton
<dl><dd>The very earth to fill the hungry mawe;</dd>
<dd>When they far'd <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a>, they fed on Fearne and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brack.html>brack</a></b>,</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:braak.html>braak</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brack.html>brack</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bracks.html>bracks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An opening caused by the parting of a solid body; a crack or breach.
<ul><li><i>c.</i> <b>1624</b>,, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Fletcher_(playwright)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Fletcher (playwright)">John <a href = vnd.unilang:fletcher.html>Fletcher</a></a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Wife_for_a_Day" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:A Wife for a Day">A Wife for a Day</a></i>, Act I, Scene 1,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.gutenberg.org/files/45780/45780-h/45780-h.htm">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>You may find time out in eternity,</dd>
<dd>Deceit and violence in heavenly Justice,</dd>
<dd>Life in the grave, and death among the blessed,</dd>
<dd><a href = vnd.unilang:ere.html>Ere</a> stain or <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brack.html>brack</a></b> in her sweet reputation.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A flaw in cloth.
<ul><li><b>1677</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hannah_Woolley" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Hannah Woolley"><a href = vnd.unilang:hannah.html>Hannah</a> Woolley</a>, <i>The Compleat Servant-Maid</i>, London: <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>. Passinger, p. 164,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://name.umdl.umich.edu/A66839.0001.001">[2]</a></sup>
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> You must take care that all the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bracks.html>bracks</a></b> and rents in the Linen be duly mended.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortening.
</p>

***bracken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bracken.html>bracken</a> (84580)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:braken.html>braken</a></i>, probably of Scandinavian origin. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">bregne</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">bräken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fern</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bracken.html>bracken</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">brackens</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of several coarse ferns, of the genus <i>Pteridium</i>, that form dense thickets; often poisonous to livestock.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An area of countryside heavily populated by this fern.</li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>brand</a> (1511)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:brant.html>brant</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>brand</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brandaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>brand</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:branden.html>branden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandje.html>brandje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>destructive, catastrophic fire <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">such as a house fire</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vreselijk.html>vreselijke</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>brand</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veroorzaakt.html>veroorzaakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doordat.html>doordat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kleuter.html>kleuter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kaarsen.html>kaarsen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:speelde.html>speelde</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That terrible <b>fire</b> originated because a toddler <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> playing with candles.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***branden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:branden.html>branden</a> (2550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:branden.html>branden</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>brand</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>. Displaced <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bernen</i>.
</p><p>The sense “to write to a storage medium” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">burn</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:branden.html>branden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive or transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to burn, to set aflame, to be alight</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of lamps and such</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be <a href = vnd.unilang:lit.html>lit</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to burn, to write to a storage medium</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***brander.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brander.html>brander</a> (20610)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:branden.html>branden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brander.html>brander</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:branders.html>branders</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandertje.html>brandertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A receptacle in which a fuel or candle <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> placed to be burnt.</li>
<li>blowtorch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fireship <span class="defdate">[from 17th c.]</span>
<ul><li>P.C. <a href = vnd.unilang:hooft.html>Hooft</a>, <i>Nederlandsche Historien</i>, Book XXII, in W. Hellinga <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> P. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brandhout.html>brandhout</a> (13679)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:branden.html>branden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hout.html>hout</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandhout.html>brandhout</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>firewood

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brandmuur.html>brandmuur</a> (119008)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>brand</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>muur</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandmuur.html>brandmuur</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandmuren.html>brandmuren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandmuur.html>brandmuurtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fire-resistant wall containing a fireplace and chimney; often dividing a residence in a front and a back section.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brandweerwagen.html>brandweerwagen</a> (44021)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandweer.html>brandweer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fire department</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wagen.html>wagen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">car, wagon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
